  DATASET
  {
    { 6966;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table14000822;
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  PackingRule@1240020000 : Record 14000715;
                                BEGIN
                                  EShipFormatAddr.BillOfLadingShipTo(ShipToAddress,"Bill of Lading");
                                  EShipFormatAddr.BillOfLadingShipFrom(ShipFromAddress,"Bill of Lading");
                                  IncludePhoneNo(ShipToAddress,"Bill of Lading"."Ship-to Phone No.");
                                  IncludePhoneNo(ShipFromAddress,"Bill of Lading"."Ship-from Phone No.");
                                  IF "Bill of Lading"."Shipping Agent Code" <> '' THEN
                                    ShippingAgent.GET("Bill of Lading"."Shipping Agent Code");
                                  CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                                  DateShipped := "Bill of Lading"."Packing Date";


                                  BillOfLadingNo := "Bill of Lading"."No.";
                                  IF PackingRule.GetPackingRule(
                                    "Bill of Lading"."Ship-to Type","Bill of Lading"."Ship-to No.","Bill of Lading"."Ship-to Code")
                                  THEN
                                    IF ("Bill of Lading"."VICS Bill of Lading No." <> '') AND
                                       (PackingRule."VICS BOL No. Prints as BOL No.")
                                    THEN
                                      BillOfLadingNo := "Bill of Lading"."VICS Bill of Lading No.";

                                  TotalPkgs := 0;
                                  TotalWeight := 0;

                                  BOLLines.RESET;
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Bill of Lading No.","No.");
                                  IF BOLLines.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      TotalPkgs := TotalPkgs + BOLLines."Packages (Top Level)";
                                      TotalWeight := TotalWeight + BOLLines.Weight;
                                    UNTIL BOLLines.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Packing Date,Released }

    { 3010;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table14000823;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Bill of Lading No.,Source Type,Source Subtype,Source ID,Type);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  LinePkgCount := 0;
                                  LinePkgWeight := 0;

                                  BOLLines.RESET;
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Bill of Lading No.","Bill of Lading No.");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source Type","Source Type");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source Subtype","Source Subtype");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source ID","Source ID");
                                  IF BOLLines.FINDLAST THEN;

                                  IF "Bill of Lading Line"."Line No." <> BOLLines."Line No." THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  BOLLines.RESET;
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Bill of Lading No.","Bill of Lading No.");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source Type","Source Type");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source Subtype","Source Subtype");
                                  BOLLines.SETRANGE(BOLLines."Source ID","Source ID");
                                  IF BOLLines.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      LinePkgCount := LinePkgCount + BOLLines."Packages (Top Level)";
                                      LinePkgWeight := LinePkgWeight + BOLLines.Weight;
                                    UNTIL BOLLines.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF "External Document No." = '' THEN
                                    "External Document No." := "Source ID";
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Bill of Lading No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1240020000;2;Column;Bill_of_Lading_Line__External_Document_No__;

    PROCEDURE IncludePhoneNo@2(VAR Address@1240030000 : ARRAY [8] OF Text[50];PhoneNo@1240030001 : Text[30]);
    VAR
      i@1240030002 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      FOR i := 1 TO 8 DO
        IF Address[i] = '' THEN BEGIN
          Address[i] := PhoneNo;
          i := 8;
        END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
